           </a>
           (2,634 metres or 8,642 feet)
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg/240px-Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg/360px-Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg/480px-Observatory_Skalnate_pleso.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           <a href="/wiki/Skalnat%C3%A9_pleso_Observatory" title="Skalnaté pleso Observatory">
            Skalnaté pleso Observatory
           </a>
           (1,751 metres or 5,745 feet)
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bystra_a4.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1932" data-file-width="2576" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Bystra_a4.jpg/240px-Bystra_a4.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Bystra_a4.jpg/360px-Bystra_a4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Bystra_a4.jpg/480px-Bystra_a4.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           <a href="/wiki/Bystr%C3%A1_(mountain)" title="Bystrá (mountain)">
            Bystrá
           </a>
           (2,248 metres or 7,375 feet)
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Tatras, with 29 peaks higher than 2,500 metres (8,202 feet)
       <a href="/wiki/Sea_level#AMSL" title="Sea level">
        AMSL
       </a>
       , are the highest mountain range in the Carpathian Mountains. Tatras occupy an area of 750 square kilometres (290 sq mi), of which the greater part 600 square kilometres (232 sq mi) lies in Slovakia. They are divided into several parts.
      </p>
      <p>
       To the north, close to the Polish border, are the
       <a href="/wiki/High_Tatras" title="High Tatras">
        High Tatras
       </a>
       which are a popular
       <a href="/wiki/Hiking" title="Hiking">
        hiking
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Skiing" title="Skiing">
        skiing
       </a>
       destination and home to many scenic lakes and valleys as well as the highest point in Slovakia, the
       <a href="/wiki/Gerlachovsk%C3%BD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt" title="Gerlachovský štít">
        Gerlachovský štít
       </a>
       at 2,655 metres (8,711 ft) and the country's highly symbolic mountain
       <a href="/wiki/Kriv%C3%A1%C5%88_(peak)" title="Kriváň (peak)">
        Kriváň
       </a>
       . To the west are the
       <a href="/wiki/Western_Tatras" title="Western Tatras">
        Western Tatras
       </a>
       with their highest peak of
       <a href="/wiki/Bystr%C3%A1_(mountain)" title="Bystrá (mountain)">
        Bystrá
       </a>
       at 2,248 metres (7,375 ft) and to the east are the
       <a href="/wiki/Belianske_Tatras" title="Belianske Tatras">
        Belianske Tatras
       </a>
       , smallest by area.
      </p>
      <p>
       Separated from the Tatras proper by the valley of the
       <a href="/wiki/V%C3%A1h" title="Váh">
        Váh
       </a>
       river are the
       <a href="/wiki/Low_Tatras" title="Low Tatras">
        Low Tatras
       </a>
       , with their highest peak of
       <a href="/wiki/%C4%8Eumbier" title="Ďumbier">
        Ďumbier
       </a>
       at 2,043 metres (6,703 ft).
      </p>
      <p>
       The Tatra mountain range is represented as one of the three hills on the
       <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Slovakia" title="Coat of arms of Slovakia">
        coat of arms of Slovakia
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="National_parks">
        National parks
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: National parks">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_national_parks_of_Slovakia" title="List of national parks of Slovakia">
        List of national parks of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Slovakia_topo.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="962" data-file-width="1400" height="241" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Slovakia_topo.jpg/350px-Slovakia_topo.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Slovakia_topo.jpg/525px-Slovakia_topo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Slovakia_topo.jpg/700px-Slovakia_topo.jpg 2x" width="350"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Slovakia_topo.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A
         <a href="/wiki/Topography" title="Topography">
          topographic
         </a>
         map of Slovakia
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       There are 9 national parks in Slovakia, they cover 6.5% of Slovak land surface.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">
        <a href="#cite_note-66">
         [65]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caves">
        Caves
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Caves">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Domica_Cave_20.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3456" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Domica_Cave_20.jpg/220px-Domica_Cave_20.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Domica_Cave_20.jpg/330px-Domica_Cave_20.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Domica_Cave_20.jpg/440px-Domica_Cave_20.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Domica_Cave_20.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Domica" title="Domica">
          Domica
         </a>
         Cave
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_caves_in_Slovakia" title="List of caves in Slovakia">
        List of caves in Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Slovakia has hundreds of caves and caverns under its mountains, of which 30 are open to the public.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">
        <a href="#cite_note-67">
         [66]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Most of the caves have
       <a href="/wiki/Stalagmite" title="Stalagmite">
        stalagmites
       </a>
       rising from the ground and
       <a href="/wiki/Stalactite" title="Stalactite">
        stalactites
       </a>
       hanging from above. There are currently five Slovak caves under
       <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">
        UNESCO
       </a>
       's World Heritage Site status. They are
       <a href="/wiki/Dob%C5%A1insk%C3%A1_Ice_Cave" title="Dobšinská Ice Cave">
        Dobšinská Ice Cave
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Domica" title="Domica">
        Domica
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Gombasek_Cave" title="Gombasek Cave">
        Gombasek Cave
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Jasovsk%C3%A1_Cave" title="Jasovská Cave">
        Jasovská Cave
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Ochtinsk%C3%A1_Aragonite_Cave" title="Ochtinská Aragonite Cave">
        Ochtinská Aragonite Cave
       </a>
       . Other caves open to the public include
       <a href="/wiki/Belianska_Cave" title="Belianska Cave">
        Belianska Cave
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Dem%C3%A4novsk%C3%A1_Cave_of_Liberty" title="Demänovská Cave of Liberty">
        Demänovská Cave of Liberty
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Dem%C3%A4novsk%C3%A1_Ice_Cave" title="Demänovská Ice Cave">
        Demänovská Ice Cave
       </a>
       or
       <a href="/wiki/Bystrianska_Cave" title="Bystrianska Cave">
        Bystrianska Cave
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rivers">
        Rivers
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Rivers">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bel%C3%A1_river_(Slovakia).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="530" data-file-width="752" height="155" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg/220px-Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg/330px-Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg/440px-Bel%C3%A1_river_%28Slovakia%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bel%C3%A1_river_(Slovakia).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Bel%C3%A1_(river)" title="Belá (river)">
          Belá River
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_rivers_of_Slovakia" title="List of rivers of Slovakia">
        List of rivers of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Most of the rivers stem in the Slovak mountains. Some only pass through and the others make a natural border with surrounding countries (more than 620 kilometres (385 mi)). For example, the
       <a href="/wiki/Dunajec" title="Dunajec">
        Dunajec
       </a>
       (17 kilometres (11 mi)) to the north, the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Danube_River" title="Danube River">
        Danube
       </a>
       (172 kilometres (107 mi)) to the south or the
       <a href="/wiki/Morava_(river)" title="Morava (river)">
        Morava
       </a>
       (119 kilometres (74 mi)) to the West. The total length of the rivers on Slovak territory is 49,774 kilometres (30,928 mi).
      </p>
      <p>
       The longest river in Slovakia is the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vah_River" title="Vah River">
        Váh
       </a>
       (403 kilometres (250 mi)), the shortest is the Čierna voda. Other important and large rivers are the
       <a href="/wiki/Myjava_(river)" title="Myjava (river)">
        Myjava
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Nitra_(river)" title="Nitra (river)">
        Nitra
       </a>
       (197 kilometres (122 mi)), the
       <a href="/wiki/Orava_(river)" title="Orava (river)">
        Orava
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Hron" title="Hron">
        Hron
       </a>
       (298 kilometres (185 mi)), the
       <a href="/wiki/Horn%C3%A1d" title="Hornád">
        Hornád
       </a>
       (193 kilometres (120 mi)), the
       <a href="/wiki/Saj%C3%B3" title="Sajó">
        Slaná
       </a>
       (110 kilometres (68 mi)), the
       <a href="/wiki/Ipe%C4%BE" title="Ipeľ">
        Ipeľ
       </a>
       (232 kilometres (144 mi), forming the border with Hungary), the
       <a href="/wiki/Bodrog" title="Bodrog">
        Bodrog
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Laborec" title="Laborec">
        Laborec
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Latorica" title="Latorica">
        Latorica
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Ondava" title="Ondava">
        Ondava
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       The biggest volume of discharge in Slovak rivers is during
       <a href="/wiki/Spring_(season)" title="Spring (season)">
        spring
       </a>
       , when the snow melts from the mountains. The only exception is the Danube, whose discharge is the greatest during summer when the snow melts in the
       <a href="/wiki/Alps" title="Alps">
        Alps
       </a>
       . The Danube is the largest river that flows through Slovakia.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">
        <a href="#cite_note-68">
         [67]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lakes">

       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">

        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>

       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dolina_Kiezmarska,_stawy_1.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg/240px-Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg/360px-Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg/480px-Dolina_Kiezmarska%2C_stawy_1.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           Zelené pleso Kežmarské
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1449" data-file-width="1932" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg/240px-Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg/360px-Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg/480px-Wielki_Hi%C5%84czowy_Staw_a1.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           <a href="/wiki/Ve%C4%BEk%C3%A9_Hincovo_pleso" title="Veľké Hincovo pleso">
            Veľké Hincovo pleso
           </a>
           is the biggest and deepest
           <a href="/wiki/Tarn_(lake)" title="Tarn (lake)">
            mountain lake
           </a>
           in the Slovak High Tatras
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="3024" data-file-width="4032" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg/240px-Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg/360px-Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg/480px-Zabie_Stawy_z_Kopy_Popradzkiej.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           Žabie pleso in the High Tatras
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 162px">
        <div style="width: 162px">
         <div class="thumb" style="width: 160px;">
          <div style="margin:0px auto;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="2736" data-file-width="3648" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg/240px-Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg/360px-Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg/480px-Zmarzly_Staw_Starolesny.jpg 2x" width="160"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="gallerytext">
          <p>
           Zbojnícke Ľadové pleso in Veľká Studená dolina
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       There are around 175 naturally formed
       <a href="/wiki/Tarn_(lake)" title="Tarn (lake)">
        tarns
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/High_Tatras" title="High Tatras">
        High Tatras
       </a>
       . With an area of 20 hectares (49 acres) and its depth of 53 metres (174 ft),
       <a href="/wiki/Ve%C4%BEk%C3%A9_Hincovo_pleso" title="Veľké Hincovo pleso">
        Veľké Hincovo pleso
       </a>
       is the largest and the deepest tarn in Slovakia. Other tarns in the High Tatras include
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0trbsk%C3%A9_pleso" title="Štrbské pleso">
        Štrbské pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Popradsk%C3%A9_pleso" title="Popradské pleso">
        Popradské pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Skalnat%C3%A9_pleso" title="Skalnaté pleso">
        Skalnaté pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Zbojn%C3%ADcke_pleso&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Zbojnícke pleso (page does not exist)">
        Zbojnícke pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Velick%C3%A9_pleso&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Velické pleso (page does not exist)">
        Velické pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%C5%BDabie_pleso&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Žabie pleso (page does not exist)">
        Žabie pleso
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Kriv%C3%A1nske_zelen%C3%A9_pleso&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Krivánske zelené pleso (page does not exist)">
        Krivánske zelené pleso
       </a>
       or
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Roh%C3%A1%C4%8Dske_ples%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Roháčske plesá (page does not exist)">
        Roháčske plesá
       </a>
       . Other than in the High Tatras there are
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Vrbick%C3%A9_pleso&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Vrbické pleso (page does not exist)">
        Vrbické pleso
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Low_Tatras" title="Low Tatras">
        Low Tatras
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Morsk%C3%A9_oko_(Slovakia)" title="Morské oko (Slovakia)">
        Morské oko
       </a>
       and
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Vinn%C3%A9_jazero&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Vinné jazero (page does not exist)">
        Vinné jazero
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Vihorlat_Mountains" title="Vihorlat Mountains">
        Vihorlat Mountains
       </a>
       or
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jezersk%C3%A9_jazero&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jezerské jazero (page does not exist)">
        Jezerské jazero
       </a>
       in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spi%C5%A1sk%C3%A1_Magura" title="Spišská Magura">
        Spišská Magura
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       The largest dams on the river Váh are
       <a href="/wiki/Liptovsk%C3%A1_Mara" title="Liptovská Mara">
        Liptovská Mara
       </a>
       and
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=S%C4%BA%C5%88ava&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sĺňava (page does not exist)">
        Sĺňava
       </a>
       . Other well-known dams are
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Oravsk%C3%A1_priehrada&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Oravská priehrada (page does not exist)">
        Oravská priehrada
       </a>
       in the north,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zempl%C3%ADnska_%C5%A0%C3%ADrava" title="Zemplínska Šírava">
        Zemplínska Šírava
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doma%C5%A1a" title="Domaša">
        Domaša
       </a>
       in the east,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Seneck%C3%A9_jazer%C3%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Senecké jazerá (page does not exist)">
        Senecké jazerá
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zlat%C3%A9_piesky" title="Zlaté piesky">
        Zlaté piesky
       </a>
       or
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Zelen%C3%A1_voda&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Zelená voda (page does not exist)">
        Zelená voda
       </a>
       in the west.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">
        Climate
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Climate">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Slovakia_koppen.svg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="648" data-file-width="765" height="186" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Slovakia_koppen.svg/220px-Slovakia_koppen.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Slovakia_koppen.svg/330px-Slovakia_koppen.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Slovakia_koppen.svg/440px-Slovakia_koppen.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Slovakia_koppen.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">
          Köppen climate classification
         </a>
         types of Slovakia
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Slovak climate lies between the temperate and
       <a href="/wiki/Continental_climate" title="Continental climate">
        continental climate
       </a>
       zones with relatively warm summers and cold, cloudy and humid winters. Temperature extremes are between −41 to 40.3 °C (−41.8 to 104.5 °F) although temperatures below −30 °C (−22 °F) are rare. The weather differs from the mountainous North to the plain South.
      </p>
      <p>
       The warmest region is
       <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
        Bratislava
       </a>
       and Southern Slovakia where the temperatures may reach 30 °C (86 °F) in summer, occasionally to 39 °C (102 °F) in
       <a href="/wiki/Hurbanovo" title="Hurbanovo">
        Hurbanovo
       </a>
       . During night, the temperatures drop to 20 °C (68 °F). The daily temperatures in winter average in the range of −5 °C (23 °F) to 10 °C (50 °F). During night it may be freezing, but usually not below −10 °C (14 °F).
      </p>
      <p>
       In Slovakia, there are
       <a href="/wiki/Season" title="Season">
        four seasons
       </a>
       , each season (Spring, Summer, Autumn and Winter) lasts three months. The dry continental air brings in the summer heat and winter frosts. In contrast, oceanic air brings rainfalls and reduces summer temperatures. In the lowlands and valleys fog is often, especially in winter.
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Spring_(season)" title="Spring (season)">
        Spring
       </a>
       starts with 21 March and is characterised by colder weather with average daily temperature of 9 °C (48 °F) in the first weeks and about 14 °C (57 °F) in May and 17 °C (63 °F) in June. In Slovakia, the weather and climate in the spring is very unstable.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:393px;max-width:393px">
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="1909" data-file-width="2488" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG/190px-CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG/285px-CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG/380px-CulHer14Slovakia328.JPG 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Summer in
          <a href="/wiki/Spi%C5%A1sk%C3%A9_Podhradie" title="Spišské Podhradie">
           Spišské Podhradie
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:197px;max-width:197px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="2736" data-file-width="3648" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG/195px-Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG/293px-Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG/390px-Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica_im_Herbst.JPG 2x" width="195"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Winter in
          <a href="/wiki/Bansk%C3%A1_%C5%A0tiavnica" title="Banská Štiavnica">
           Banská Štiavnica
          </a>
          ; the town is a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site" title="UNESCO World Heritage Site">
           UNESCO World Heritage Site
          </a>
          .
         </div>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:left">
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Summer" title="Summer">
        Summer
       </a>
       starts on 22 June and is usually characterised by hot weather with daily temperatures exceeding 30 °C (86 °F). July is the warmest month with temperatures up to about 37 to 40 °C (99 to 104 °F), especially in regions of southern Slovakia – in the urban area of Komárno, Hurbanovo or Štúrovo. Showers or thunderstorms may occur because of the summer monsoon called Medardova kvapka (Medard drop – 40 days of rain). Summer in Northern Slovakia is usually mild with temperatures around 25 °C (77 °F) (less in the mountains).
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Autumn" title="Autumn">
        Autumn
       </a>
       in Slovakia starts on 23 September and is mostly characterised by wet weather and wind, although the first weeks can be very warm and sunny. The average temperature in September is around 14 °C (57 °F), in November to 3 °C (37 °F). Late September and early October is a dry and sunny time of year (so-called Indian Summer).
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Winter" title="Winter">
        Winter
       </a>
       starts on 21 December with temperatures around −5 to −10 °C (23 to 14 °F). In December and January it is usually snowing, these are the coldest months of the year. At lower altitudes, snow does not stay the whole winter, it is changing into the thaw and frost. Winters are colder in the mountains, where the snow usually lasts until March or April and the night temperatures fall to −20 °C (−4 °F) and colder.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">
        <a href="#cite_note-69">
         [68]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Biodiversity">
        Biodiversity
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Biodiversity">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Endemic_Plant_Species_in_Slovakia" title="Endemic Plant Species in Slovakia">
        Endemic Plant Species in Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry,_Dolina_Bielej_vody,_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_(32).JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2481" data-file-width="3119" height="175" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG/220px-Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG/330px-Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG/440px-Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry%2C_Dolina_Bielej_vody%2C_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_%2832%29.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vysok%C3%A9_Tatry,_Dolina_Bielej_vody,_cestou_od_Zelen%C3%A9ho_plesa_na_Jah%C5%88ac%C3%AD_%C5%A1t%C3%ADt_(32).JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <i>
          Rupicapra rupicapra tatrica
         </i>
         in the
         <a href="/wiki/Tatra_Mountains" title="Tatra Mountains">
          Tatra Mountains
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Slovakia signed the Rio
       <a href="/wiki/Convention_on_Biological_Diversity" title="Convention on Biological Diversity">
        Convention on Biological Diversity
       </a>
       on 19 May 1993, and became a party to the convention on 25 August 1994.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">
        <a href="#cite_note-70">
         [69]
        </a>
       </sup>
       It has subsequently produced a
       <a href="/wiki/Biodiversity_action_plan" title="Biodiversity action plan">
        National Biodiversity Strategy and Action Plan
       </a>
       , which was received by the convention on 2 November 1998.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">
        <a href="#cite_note-71">
         [70]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The biodiversity of Slovakia comprises animals (such as annellids, arthropods, molluscs, nematodes and vertebrates), fungi (
       <a href="/wiki/Ascomycota" title="Ascomycota">
        Ascomycota
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Basidiomycota" title="Basidiomycota">
        Basidiomycota
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Chytridiomycota" title="Chytridiomycota">
        Chytridiomycota
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Glomeromycota" title="Glomeromycota">
        Glomeromycota
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Zygomycota" title="Zygomycota">
        Zygomycota
       </a>
       ), micro-organisms (including
       <a href="/wiki/Mycetozoa" title="Mycetozoa">
        Mycetozoa
       </a>
       ), and plants.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Fungi">
        Fungi
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Fungi">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Over 4000 species of fungi have been recorded from Slovakia.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">
        <a href="#cite_note-72">
         [71]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">
        <a href="#cite_note-73">
         [72]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Of these, nearly 1500 are lichen-forming species.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">
        <a href="#cite_note-74">
         [73]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Some of these fungi are undoubtedly endemic, but not enough is known to say how many. Of the lichen-forming species, about 40% have been classified as threatened in some way. About 7% are apparently extinct, 9% endangered, 17% vulnerable, and 7% rare. The conservation status of non-lichen-forming fungi in Slovakia is not well documented, but there is a red list for its larger fungi.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">
        <a href="#cite_note-75">
         [74]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Politics_and_government">
        Politics and government
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Politics and government">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main articles:
       <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Slovakia" title="Politics of Slovakia">
        Politics of Slovakia
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Law_of_Slovakia" title="Law of Slovakia">
        Law of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Slovakia" title="Prime Minister of Slovakia">
        Prime Minister of Slovakia
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Slovakia" title="List of Presidents of Slovakia">
        List of Presidents of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Grassalkovich_Palace_(2).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1776" data-file-width="5561" height="128" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg/400px-Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg/600px-Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg/800px-Grassalkovich_Palace_%282%29.jpg 2x" width="400"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Grassalkovich_Palace_(2).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Grassalkovich_Palace" title="Grassalkovich Palace">
          Grassalkovich Palace
         </a>
         in
         <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
          Bratislava
         </a>
         is the seat of the
         <a href="/wiki/President_of_Slovakia" title="President of Slovakia">
          President of Slovakia
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:194px;max-width:194px">
        <div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bratislava,_Parlament,_Slovensko.jpg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg/190px-Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg/285px-Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg/380px-Bratislava%2C_Parlament%2C_Slovensko.jpg 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          The
          <a href="/wiki/National_Council_(Slovakia)" title="National Council (Slovakia)">
           National Council
          </a>
          building in
          <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
           Bratislava
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bratislava,_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c,_Slovensko.jpg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4153" height="130" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg/190px-Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg/285px-Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg/380px-Bratislava%2C_Letn%C3%BD_arcibiskupsk%C3%BD_pal%C3%A1c%2C_Slovensko.jpg 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          <a href="/wiki/Episcopal_Summer_Palace,_Bratislava" title="Episcopal Summer Palace, Bratislava">
           Episcopal Summer Palace
          </a>
          , the seat of the
          <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Slovakia" title="Government of Slovakia">
           government of Slovakia
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Slovakia is a
       <a href="/wiki/Parliamentary_system" title="Parliamentary system">
        parliamentary democratic
       </a>
       republic with a
       <a href="/wiki/Multi-party_system" title="Multi-party system">
        multi-party system
       </a>
       . The last
       <a href="/wiki/Slovak_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Slovak parliamentary election, 2016">
        parliamentary elections
       </a>
       were held on 5 March 2016 and two rounds of
       <a href="/wiki/Slovak_presidential_election,_2014" title="Slovak presidential election, 2014">
        presidential elections
       </a>
       took place on 15 and 29 March 2014.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Slovak
       <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">
        head of state
       </a>
       and the formal head of the executive is the president (currently
       <a href="/wiki/Andrej_Kiska" title="Andrej Kiska">
        Andrej Kiska
       </a>
       ), though with very limited powers. The president is elected by direct, popular vote under the
       <a href="/wiki/Two-round_system" title="Two-round system">
        two-round system
       </a>
       for a five-year term. Most
       <a href="/wiki/Executive_(government)" title="Executive (government)">
        executive
       </a>
       power lies with the
       <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">
        head of government
       </a>
       , the prime minister (currently
       <a href="/wiki/Robert_Fico" title="Robert Fico">
        Robert Fico
       </a>
       ), who is usually the leader of the winning party, but he/she needs to form a majority coalition in the parliament. The prime minister is appointed by the president. The remainder of the cabinet is appointed by the president on the recommendation of the prime minister.
      </p>
      <p>
       Slovak highest
       <a href="/wiki/Legislature" title="Legislature">
        legislative
       </a>
       body is the 150-seat
       <a href="/wiki/Unicameralism" title="Unicameralism">
        unicameral
       </a>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Council_of_the_Slovak_Republic" title="National Council of the Slovak Republic">
        National Council of the Slovak Republic
       </a>
       (
       <i>
        Národná rada Slovenskej republiky
       </i>
       ). Delegates are elected for a four-year term on the basis of
       <a href="/wiki/Proportional_representation" title="Proportional representation">
        proportional representation
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Slovak highest
       <a href="/wiki/Judiciary" title="Judiciary">
        judicial body
       </a>
       is the
       <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Slovakia" title="Constitutional Court of Slovakia">
        Constitutional Court of Slovakia
       </a>
       (
       <i>
        Ústavný súd
       </i>
       ), which rules on constitutional issues. The 13 members of this court are appointed by the president from a slate of candidates nominated by parliament.
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Slovakia" title="Constitution of Slovakia">
        Constitution of the Slovak Republic
       </a>
       was ratified 1 September 1992, and became effective 1 January 1993. It was amended in September 1998 to allow
       <a href="/wiki/Direct_election" title="Direct election">
        direct election
       </a>
       of the president and again in February 2001 due to EU admission requirements. The
       <a href="/wiki/Civil_law_(legal_system)" title="Civil law (legal system)">
        civil law system
       </a>
       is based on Austro-Hungarian codes. The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Code_(law)" title="Code (law)">
        legal code
       </a>
       was modified to comply with the obligations of
       <a href="/wiki/Organization_for_Security_and_Co-operation_in_Europe" title="Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe">
        Organization on Security and Cooperation in Europe
       </a>
       (OSCE) and to expunge the
       <a href="/wiki/Marxism%E2%80%93Leninism" title="Marxism–Leninism">
        Marxist–Leninist
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Law" title="Law">
        legal theory
       </a>
       . Slovakia accepts the compulsory
       <a href="/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice" title="International Court of Justice">
        International Court of Justice
       </a>
       jurisdiction with reservations.
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Foreign_relations">
        Foreign relations
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Foreign relations">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Slovakia" title="Foreign relations of Slovakia">
        Foreign relations of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Slovakia" title="List of diplomatic missions of Slovakia">
        List of diplomatic missions of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:405px;max-width:405px">
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bratislava,_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="1701" data-file-width="2551" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG/190px-Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG/285px-Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG/380px-Bratislava%2C_the_Japanese_Embassy.JPG 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Embassy of
          <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">
           Japan
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
           Bratislava
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:209px;max-width:209px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="1393" data-file-width="2271" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg/207px-SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg/311px-SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg/414px-SlovakianEmbassyWashingtonDC01.jpg 2x" width="207"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Slovak Embassy in
          <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">
           Washington, D.C.
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:left">
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Slovakia joined the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">
        NATO
       </a>
       in 2004 and the
       <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">
        Eurozone
       </a>
       in 2009.
      </p>
      <p>
       Slovakia is a member of the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
        United Nations
       </a>
       (since 1993) and participates in its specialised agencies. The country was, on 10 October 2005, elected to a two-year term on the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">
        UN Security Council
       </a>
       from 2006 to 2007. It is also a member of the
       <a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">
        Schengen Area
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Europe" title="Council of Europe">
        Council of Europe
       </a>
       (CoE), the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Organization_for_Security_and_Cooperation_in_Europe" title="Organization for Security and Cooperation in Europe">
        Organization for Security and Cooperation in Europe
       </a>
       (OSCE), the
       <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">
        World Trade Organization
       </a>
       (WTO), the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Organisation_for_Economic_Co-operation_and_Development" title="Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development">
        Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development
       </a>
       (OECD), the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_Organization_for_Nuclear_Research" title="European Organization for Nuclear Research">
        European Organization for Nuclear Research
       </a>
       (CERN) and part of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Visegrad_Four" title="Visegrad Four">
        Visegrad Four
       </a>
       (V4, Slovakia,
       <a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">
        Hungary
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">
        Czech Republic
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">
        Poland
       </a>
       ).
      </p>
      <p>
       The Slovak Republic and the Czech Republic entered into a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Customs_Union" title="Customs Union">
        Customs Union
       </a>
       upon the division of Czechoslovakia in 1993, which facilitates a relatively free flow of goods and services.
      </p>
      <p>
       Slovakia maintains
       <a href="/wiki/Diplomacy" title="Diplomacy">
        diplomatic relations
       </a>
       with 134 countries, primarily through its
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Slovakia)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Slovakia)">
        Ministry of Foreign Affairs
       </a>
       . As of December 2013, Slovakia maintained 90 missions abroad, including 64 embassies, seven missions to multilateral organisations, nine consulates-general, one consular office, one Slovak Economic and Cultural Office and eight Slovak Institutes.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">
        <a href="#cite_note-76">
         [75]
        </a>
       </sup>
       There are 44 embassies and 35 honorary consulates in
       <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
        Bratislava
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Military">
        Military
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Military">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Slovakia" title="Military of Slovakia">
        Military of Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:388px;max-width:388px">
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="2250" data-file-width="3000" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG/190px-Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG/285px-Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG/380px-Slovak_Air_Force_MiG-29AS.JPG 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Slovak Air Force
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MiG-29" title="MiG-29">
           MiG-29
          </a>
          NATO upgrade
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:192px;max-width:192px">
         <div class="thumbimage">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="459" data-file-width="612" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg/190px-Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg/285px-Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg/380px-Slovak_Army_5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_in_Afghanistan2.jpg 2x" width="190"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">
          Slovak 5th Special Forces Regiment operating in eastern Afghanistan
         </div>
        </div>
        <div style="clear:left">
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Armed Forces of the Slovak Republic number 14,000 uniformed personnel.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">
        <a href="#cite_note-77">
         [76]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Slovakia joined
       <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">
        NATO
       </a>
       in March 2004.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">
        <a href="#cite_note-78">
         [77]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The country has been an active participant in US- and NATO-led military actions. There is a joint Czech-Slovak peacekeeping force in Kosovo. From 2006 the army transformed into a fully professional organisation and compulsory military service was abolished.
      </p>
      <p>
       Slovak
       <a href="/wiki/Ground_Forces_of_the_Slovak_Republic" title="Ground Forces of the Slovak Republic">
        Ground Forces
       </a>
       are made up of two active
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mechanised_infantry" title="Mechanised infantry">
        mechanised infantry
       </a>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brigades" title="Brigades">
        brigades
       </a>
       . The
       <a href="/wiki/Slovak_Air_Force" title="Slovak Air Force">
        Air and Air Defence Forces
       </a>
       comprise one
       <a href="/wiki/Wing_(military_aviation_unit)" title="Wing (military aviation unit)">
        wing
       </a>
       of
       <a href="/wiki/Fighter_aircraft" title="Fighter aircraft">
        fighters
       </a>
       , one wing of utility
       <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">
        helicopters
       </a>
       , and one SAM brigade. Training and support forces comprise a National Support Element (Multifunctional Battalion, Transport Battalion, Repair Battalion), a garrison force of the capital city Bratislava, as well as a training battalion, and various logistics and communication and information bases. Miscellaneous forces under the direct command of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Staff" title="General Staff">
        General Staff
       </a>
       include the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/5th_Special_Forces_Regiment_(Slovakia)" title="5th Special Forces Regiment (Slovakia)">
        5th Special Forces Regiment
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Human_rights">
        Human rights
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Human rights">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The US State Department in 2015 reported:
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        "The government generally respected the human rights of its citizens; however, there were problems in some areas. Notable human rights problems included official corruption; a judiciary that was inefficient and engendered low public trust; and widespread discrimination against Roma minority. Other human rights problems included: excessive use of police force against migrants, physical mistreatment of detainees; lack of independent oversight of police; targeting of the press for civil defamation suits by members of the political, judicial, and financial elite; expressions of anti-Semitism by right-wing groups; and demeaning statements and demonstrations against refugees and migrants."
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">
         <a href="#cite_note-79">
          [78]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       Human rights in Slovakia are guaranteed by the
       <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Slovakia" title="Constitution of Slovakia">
        Constitution of Slovakia
       </a>
       from the year 1992 and by multiple international laws signed in Slovakia between 1948 and 2006.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">
        <a href="#cite_note-80">
         [79]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Slovakia
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slovak_nationality_law" title="Slovak nationality law">
        excludes multiple citizenships
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">
        Administrative divisions
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Slovakia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Administrative divisions">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main articles:
       <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_Slovakia" title="Regions of Slovakia">
        Regions of Slovakia
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Districts_of_Slovakia" title="Districts of Slovakia">
        Districts of Slovakia
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_municipalities_and_towns_in_Slovakia" title="List of municipalities and towns in Slovakia">
        List of municipalities and towns in Slovakia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2230" data-file-width="4080" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg/220px-Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg/330px-Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg/440px-Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bratislava_Cityscape.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">
          Bratislava
         </a>
         , capital and largest city of Slovakia
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       As for
       <a href="/wiki/Administrative_division" title="Administrative division">
        administrative division
       </a>
       , Slovakia is subdivided into 8
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Kraj" title="Kraj">
         krajov
        </a>
       </i>
       (singular –
       <i>
        kraj
       </i>
       , usually translated as "region"), each of which is named after its principal city. Regions have enjoyed a certain degree of autonomy since 2002. Their
       <a href="/wiki/Self-governance" title="Self-governance">
        self-governing
       </a>
       bodies are referred to as Self-governing (or autonomous) Regions (sg.
       <i>
        samosprávny kraj
       </i>
       , pl.
       <i>
        samosprávne kraje
       </i>
       ) or Upper-Tier Territorial Units (sg.
       <i>
        vyšší územný celok
       </i>
       , pl.
       <i>
        vyššie územné celky
       </i>
       , abbr. VÚC).
      </p>
      <p>
       The "kraje" are subdivided into many
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Okres" title="Okres">
         okresy
        </a>
       </i>
       (sg.
       <i>
        okres
       </i>
       , usually translated as counties). Slovakia currently has 79 districts.
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <i>
        okresy
       </i>
       are further divided into
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/List_of_municipalities_and_towns_in_Slovakia" title="List of municipalities and towns in Slovakia">
         obcí
        </a>
       </i>
       (sg.
       <i>
        obec
       </i>
       , usually translated as "municipality"). There are currently 2,891 obcí.
      </p>
      <p>
       In terms of economics and
       <a href="/wiki/Unemployment" title="Unemployment">
        unemployment
       </a>
       rate, the western regions are richer than eastern regions. Bratislava is the third richest region of the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       by GDP (PPP) per capita (after
       <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">
        Hamburg
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_City" title="Luxembourg City">
        Luxembourg City
       </a>
       ), GDP at purchasing power parity is about three times higher than in other Slovak regions.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-finweb.hnonline.sk_81-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-finweb.hnonline.sk-81">
         [80]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">
        <a href="#cite_note-82">
         [81]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <table style="width:98%; background:none;">
       <tr>

             <img alt="Žilina Erb.svg" data-file-height="289" data-file-width="268" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg/14px-%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg/21px-%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg/28px-%C5%BDilina_Erb.svg.png 2x" width="14"/>
            </a>
            <a href="/wiki/%C5%BDilina" title="Žilina">
             Žilina
            </a>
           </td>
           <td align="right">
            688,851
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <a href="/wiki/Ko%C5%A1ice_Region" title="Košice Region">
             Košice Region
            </a>

            <i>
             Košický kraj
            </i>
           </td>
           <td>
            <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_arms_of_Ko%C5%A1ice.png">

             Prešovský kraj
            </i>

            <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg">
             <img alt="Coa Slovakia Town Eperjes.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="260" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg/14px-Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg/21px-Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg/28px-Coa_Slovakia_Town_Eperjes.svg.png 2x" width="14"/>

         </table>
